`0.5980*P - 0.5980*P²/32.94 + 0.5980*P - 0.5980*P*exp(-0.0768*P)`

`1.196*P - 0.01815*P² - 0.5980*P*exp(-0.0768*P)`

So GT = `c_a*P² + c_b*P + c_c*P*exp(c_d*P)` where:
- c_a = -0.01815
- c_b = 1.196
- c_c = -0.5980
- c_d = -0.0768

The GT is a function of P only (no t dependence). This means any t-dependent terms in candidates must have their coefficients set to 0.

**Key structure needed:** `P² * const + P * const + P * exp(P * const) * const`

Let me check candidates that can reduce to this form:

- c5 = 1.196
- c3 = -0.5980
- c4 = -0.0768

Yes! This works perfectly.
